posted:Posted March 12, 2024
msg:We were delighted to find that our room was spacious and provided ample space for us to relax and unwind. The reading lounge in the room was a lovely addition, allowing us to enjoy some quiet reading time. The bathroom is spacious and clean.

The check-in staff were friendly and willing to assist us with any inquiries or requests we had. The helpfulness and courteousness made the check-in process smooth and welcoming.

Convenient Location: The hotel's location was truly advantageous, as it was within walking distance of Zhongyang Street, which is known as Asia's longest pedestrian street. This central location allowed us to easily explore and enjoy the vibrant atmosphere of Harbin.

The inclusion of breakfast buffet and afternoon tea was a delightful addition to our stay. The hotel offered a decent selection of food during both meals, ensuring that we had a satisfying start to our day and a pleasant afternoon treat.

Staff at the restaurant were always attentive and ready to assist us. They provided excellent service and ensured that our dining experience was enjoyable. Their attentiveness added an extra touch of warmth and hospitality to our meals.

City Tour Arrangements: We were pleased to discover that the hotel had a local tour arranger at the lobby near the reception area. Ms. Tong Tong, the tour arranger, proved to be extremely helpful in organizing a private car for our city tour. She ensured that our preferences were taken into account and made valuable suggestions for places to explore.

Professional and Polite Driver: Our driver for the city tour, Mr. Gwu MiAn, was exceptional in his professionalism and attentiveness. He took us to the places we wanted to visit and made sure we were comfortable throughout the journey. His kind and polite demeanor, coupled with his provision of water to keep us hydrated, added an extra level of comfort to our city tour.

Overall, our stay at was memorable and enjoyable. The spacious rooms, clean bathroom, helpful check-in staff, convenient location, inclusion of breakfast buffet and afternoon tea with decent selections, and the attentive restaurant staff all contributed to a positive experience. We highly recommend this hotel to anyone visiting Harbin and seeking a comfortable and convenient stay.

posted:Posted January 15, 2023
msg:The hotel is located just outside the busy pedestrian street, very convenient and easy access to the city and most tourist sights.

The room was spacious and comfortable, the bed was quite large and soft but the pillows were a little hard and thin.

A common feature of new hotels is the inability to turn off individual lights, and rather select "moods" or settings, this is useful when you're waking up in the morning or or looking for different lighting, but i could not figure out how to turn on the bathroom lights without turning on all lights, which was quite troublesome.

The hotel room seemed as though it had not been cleaned thoroughly, there was some dust on the table and floor, and the bath had a layer of dust. It was not too bad, so it was easy enough to clean myself.

Overall it was a good hotel with a good stay, the staff are friendly and efficient, the location is great, and for the price it was well worth it.

posted:Posted January 9, 2023
msg:The Hotel itself is nice and the rooms big and spacious. The bed was extremely comfortable and the room had a bathtub, which was great for a relaxed evening after having spend the whole day outside in the cold. 
The staff at the reception were very kind and spoke English, which made it easy to communicate. 
The location is great, just a few meters away from central avenue and a short walking distance away from St. Sophia Cathedral.
The room itself could have been a little cleaner in my personal opinion (surfaces, the carpet, etc.), but all in all it was a nice room. 
The breakfast was really basic and did not have a lot of options unfortunately. 
One thing that really bothered me: the walls in the rooms seem to be very thin, there was a lot of noise coming from the hallway and other rooms (loud music, voices, people shouting, etc.), which was very annoying and made it hard to fall asleep. 
All in all I would probably stay in the Huate Hotel again, if I should ever come back to Harbin, as the price/performance ratio is alright.

The hotel is very close to Central Street, that is, a distance of twenty or thirty meters. It is very convenient to eat and go shopping. There are also several bus stops at the door, and the traffic is convenient.

Although the hotel lobby is not as big as a five-star hotel, it is clean and bright. The service attitude is good. The hotel room is very large. We live as two adults and one child, and feel very comfortable.

The sink and bathtub are outside, and the bathroom and toilet are separate. fine. The bed is also quite big.

After we checked into the hotel, we went out for a stroll, and when we came back at night, we saw snacks, yogurt, and steam eye masks on the table.

The water provided by the hotel is a small bottle of Baisui Mountain. If you think it is not enough, you can tell the waiter. The waiter will generously bring you five or six bottles, and then enthusiastically ask you if it is enough, and then bring it to you.

Personally, I think the afternoon tea provided is tasteless, just two or three kinds of fruits and several kinds of tea. Several small biscuits.
